Claim Clash Alpha - Change Logs
================================
Last updated: June 30, 2026
Current source version: 0.1.91 Beta
Current packaged build in dist: 0.1.89 Beta

Thank you for testing. Below is everything that changed in recent iterations.


HOUSEKEEPING (June 27, 2026)
----------------------------
- Renamed UPDATE-NOTES.txt to CHANGE LOGS.txt.
- CHANGE LOGS auto-updates on each iteration bump (build-with-checksum.ps1).
- Tester zip packages now include TROUBLESHOOTING.txt for exe launch issues.



VERSION 0.1.71
--------------
The Brain (hidden background AI)
  - Background system fetches today's headlines and generates a daily controversial-topic question.
  - Load Example Flow alternates: random static question, then daily Brain question, then random, and so on.
  - Rapid clicks on the Brain turn wait silently until the daily question is ready.
  - Brain questions persist in a 300-item pool (oldest removed when full).
  - Brain uses Primary AI with free-tier fallback; separate hidden session from the main answer box.

Brain security
  - Every Brain session opens with a creator-authority security rule (no legal name in prompt).
  - Every Brain API call reinforces a short non-negotiable security prefix.
  - User game input is never passed to The Brain as instructions.

Setup screen
  - API key / plan link button beside each key field (setup screen only).
  - Red/green dot on the Primary AI row shows API availability (checked on launch).


VERSION 0.1.72
--------------
Security: separate Alpha vs Release build profiles
  - API keys removed from index.html source.
  - Alpha builds: scripts/set-build-profile.ps1 -Profile Alpha (used by build-with-checksum.ps1).
  - Release/Store builds: scripts/build-release.ps1 sets Release profile with no embedded keys.
  - Default committed build-profile.js is Release (empty keys).
  - Alpha agreement and pre-filled key UI hidden on Release builds.


VERSION 0.1.73
--------------
Security: Cast-to-TV XSS hardening
  - Question text on the TV mirror is plain text only (strips pasted HTML).
  - Primary and comparison AI answers use a sanitized HTML allowlist (formatting tags only).
  - AI names and bookmarks use textContent, not raw innerHTML concatenation.


VERSION 0.1.74
--------------
Security: plain-text API payloads and recall sanitization
  - All AI API calls now read the question box as plain text (getQuestionPlainText), not HTML.
  - Grok browser, comparison queries, bookmarks, and primary Ask use plain text payloads.
  - Past session recall strips HTML and drops injection-like lines from saved export excerpts.
  - Recall context includes an explicit untrusted-data security preamble for the primary AI.
  - Past Sessions "Use in question" sets textContent instead of innerHTML.


VERSION 0.1.75
--------------
Security: Cast-to-TV pairing and LAN-only bind
  - Cast server binds to your LAN IP only (not 0.0.0.0 / all interfaces).
  - Each cast session gets a random 8-character pairing code in the URL.
  - /state, mirror page, QR, and assets require a valid token (403 otherwise).
  - TVs that open IP:Port only see a pairing code entry screen (cast-pairing.html).
  - Cast modal shows the pairing code and updated connection instructions.
  - Removed wildcard CORS headers from cast responses.


VERSION 0.1.76
--------------
Security: Brain localStorage validation
  - Integrity hash checked on raw load before sanitization (tampered data is wiped).
  - Question pool, daily question, and session messages sanitized on load and save.
  - Pool entries and daily questions must pass length, injection-pattern, and HTML-stripping checks.
  - AI-generated daily questions and pool additions run through the same sanitizer before persisting.
  - Load Example Flow re-validates the daily Brain question before showing it in the question box.
  - Brain example questions use textContent (not innerHTML) in the question box.
  - Stale daily-date rollover now updates integrity hash via saveDaily().


VERSION 0.1.77
--------------
Security: Microsoft Store MSIX prep and privacy policy
  - Added PRIVACY-POLICY.md (required for Store listing and AI network use).
  - distribution/PRIVACY-POLICY.txt for offline reference and tester packages.
  - About modal Privacy Policy link opens the configured HTTPS URL.
  - privacyPolicyUrl in version.json syncs to the app via sync-version.ps1.
  - Fixed tauri.store.conf.json: MSI + offline WebView2 (Tauri does not bundle native MSIX).
  - scripts/build-store.ps1 builds Release Store MSI to dist/.
  - MICROSOFT_STORE.md updated with enrollment, capabilities, and silent-install steps.


VERSION 0.1.78
--------------
Security: server-side Brain (creator-only control)
  - Daily Brain questions now come only from a creator-signed HTTPS JSON feed.
  - Rust verifies Ed25519 signatures before the app accepts any Brain content.
  - Removed client-side RSS + user-API Brain generation (users cannot author Brain tasks locally).
  - brain-feed/ folder: draft.json, signed feed.json, public.key.hex, README.
  - scripts/generate-brain-keys.mjs and scripts/sign-brain-feed.mjs for creator publishing.
  - version.json brainFeedUrl + brainVerifyPublicKeyHex sync to src-tauri/src/brain_config.rs.
  - Load Example Flow Brain turn uses signed feed only; skips silently if feed unavailable.
  - Private signing key gitignored; only public key ships in the app.

CREATOR SETUP (required for Brain daily questions)
  1. Set brainFeedUrl in version.json to your hosted feed.json URL and push brain-feed/feed.json to GitHub.
  2. Run node scripts/sign-brain-feed.mjs after editing brain-feed/draft.json each day.
  3. Rebuild or sync-version after URL/key changes.


VERSION 0.1.79
--------------
Export filename format (ClaimsClash)
  - New pattern: ClaimsClash [version] [date] [convo] [topic].ext
  - Example: ClaimsClash v1 2026-06-27 01 Panama Canal Treaties.pdf
  - Re-export same session bumps version (v2, v3...) for same date + convo + topic.
  - New session same day gets next convo number (01, 02, 03...).
  - Version and convo auto-detected from existing files in Documents\Claim Clash Sessions\.
  - Save As pre-fills suggested topic; edit the topic segment before saving.
  - Email attach and Markdown backup use the same naming. Legacy conv N files still parse for recall.


VERSION 0.1.80
--------------
Setup: API status dot
  - Primary AI row shows a live status dot (green / red / amber / blue for browser-only Grok).
  - Dot waits until the provider row is in the DOM before rendering (fixes missing dot on launch).
  - Legend on the setup screen explains each color.

Load Example Flow: rule of 4
  - Clicks 1, 2, and 3 load stock example questions; click 4 tries the daily Brain question.
  - If the Brain feed is unavailable on click 4, a stock question is used instead.

Steelman rules
  - Rules walkthrough includes a Steelman vs Strawman section.
  - Hidden steelman directive augments primary AI calls to encourage strongest-counterargument framing.


VERSION 0.1.81
--------------
Built for two (positioning and UI)
  - Welcome, rules, main game, About, and feedback copy emphasize two players at one screen.
  - Solo mode remains available but is clearly optional for testing alone.
  - HOW-TO-TEST and alpha agreement updated for partner-first play.
  - Short description: "Built for two: evidence-based questions with a shared AI".

Grade level (academic use)
  - Setup and Settings let you pick a US grade band or map international grades to US bands.
  - Hidden directive adjusts reading level and inquiry framing (no IQ gate).
  - See GRADE-LEVEL-NOTES.txt (creator file, not in tester zip).

Primary AI: paid-plan guidance
  - Amber banners on setup, settings, and game screen recommend paid API plans for primary AI.
  - OpenRouter primary defaults to paid models first when primary is starred.
  - Session help text updated for two-player quota realities.

Email provider freeze fix
  - Feedback modal stays open when switching email providers.
  - Native attach uses a detached PowerShell path (no blocking Outlook COM freeze).
  - Saved attachment file is reused when you switch providers mid-send.


VERSION 0.1.83
--------------
Installation program - Step 2: NSIS setup installer
  - Root cause: NSIS cannot read scripts under C:\Windows\System32 (WoW64 path rules).
  - Added scripts/build-nsis-installer.ps1 - stages to ClaimClash\claim-clash-tv-build, bundles NSIS, copies setup to dist/.
  - build-with-checksum.ps1 auto-uses staging when source is under System32.
  - Drive zip now includes Claim Clash {version} - Setup.exe.
  - HOW-TO-INSTALL.txt: Option A is NSIS setup; PowerShell script is Option B.
  - Verified: dist\Claim Clash 0.1.82 Alpha - Setup.exe


VERSION 0.1.82
--------------

Step 1: stabilized portable build
  - Documented 0.1.80 and 0.1.81 changes in this changelog (were missing at package time).
  - Rebuilt portable exe + SHA-256 checksum in dist/.
  - Tester Drive zip repackaged with HOW-TO-TEST, TROUBLESHOOTING, agreement, and changelog.
  - NSIS installer fixed in Step 2 via staging build (see 0.1.83 notes).
  - Portable exe verified: dist\Claim Clash 0.1.82 Alpha.exe

Build pipeline (scratch rebuild)
  - Added build-from-scratch.ps1: cargo clean, sync without bump, portable-only (--no-bundle).
  - build-with-checksum.ps1 now supports -Clean, -NoIncrement, and -PortableOnly flags.
  - Scratch builds use -PortableOnly; full NSIS via scripts/build-nsis-installer.ps1.

VERSION 0.1.91
--------------
Release vs developer testing builds
  - Main build (dist/): Release profile — no embedded API keys, rules walkthrough "do not show again" resets when switching from Dev, free-tier comparison AIs only by default (Gemini, Groq, OpenRouter, Grok).
  - Dev build (ClaimClash/beta-dev/): Dev profile — pre-filled keys from alpha-keys.local.json, keeps your saved settings.
  - Every normal build updates BOTH together: build-with-checksum.ps1, build-release.ps1, build-both.ps1, build-from-scratch.ps1 (use -SkipDev only to skip beta-dev).
  - beta-dev also receives CHANGE LOGS.txt alongside the Dev exe.


VERSION 0.1.90
--------------
Load Example: "current events question" wording
  - Renamed player-facing "timely question" copy to "current events question" (button, hint, rules walkthrough).
  - Click 2 still loads today's signed feed question once per session (Rule of 2 unchanged).

Brain feed
  - Updated 2026-06-30 daily question to Supreme Court term-closing rulings (dominant news/social topic).
  - Added scripts/craft-current-events-question.mjs to draft questions from top headlines via Gemini.


VERSION 0.1.89
--------------
Load Example: Rule of 2 restored
  - Click 1 loads a stock preloaded example.
  - Click 2 loads today's timely question from the signed feed (once per session).
  - After click 2, Load Example serves stock examples only until you start a new session.
  - New session resets the Rule of 2 counter.

User-facing wording
  - Removed Rule of 4 copy from Load Example button, hint, and rules walkthrough.
  - No "Brain" label in player-facing Load Example text (timely question wording only).
  - Paid-plan tip remains behind the (i) notice button on the game screen.

FILENAME FORMAT (0.1.79 and later)
----------------------------------
All exports use: ClaimsClash [version] [date] [convo] [topic].ext

Examples:
  ClaimsClash v1 2026-06-27 01 [topic].pdf
  ClaimsClash v1 2026-06-27 02 AI Ethics Debate.md
  ClaimsClash v2 2026-06-27 01 Panama Canal Treaties.pdf   (re-export)
  ClaimsClash v1 2026-06-27 01 [topic] part 2 of 3.pdf   (multi-part email)

version = export version for this convo/topic (v1, v2, v3...).
date = YYYY-MM-DD (export date).
convo = sequential conversation number for that date (01, 02, 03...).
topic = suggested from first question, or [topic] to edit on Save As.


VERSION 0.1.58
--------------
Rules walkthrough
  - After the welcome screen, Next walks through 8 rules topics before you enter the game.
  - Checkbox to skip the walkthrough on future launches.
  - Start Claim Clash appears after the final rules screen.


VERSION 0.1.59
--------------
Export Session
  - New Export Session button in Quick Actions.
  - Choose Markdown (.md), Word (.docx), or PDF (.pdf).
  - Exports include primary AI conversation, bookmarks, and comparison responses on screen.


VERSION 0.1.60 through 0.1.63
-----------------------------
Email export
  - Email this export from the Export Session modal.
  - Attach file or Text only (full summary in email body; large sessions split into parts).
  - Gmail, Outlook, Yahoo, iCloud, and Default app buttons.

PDF and email stability
  - Fixed hangs and crashes when exporting long sessions as PDF for email.
  - Safer PDF generation with timeout and Markdown fallback when needed.
  - Large sessions split into multiple attachment parts automatically.


VERSION 0.1.64
--------------
Automatic Markdown backup
  - Save File also saves a Markdown backup to Documents\Claim Clash Sessions\.
  - Backup uses the same session content as your export.


VERSION 0.1.65
--------------
Export filenames and email attach
  - Files use conv N - [topic] naming (see format above).
  - Email attach tries Outlook or Thunderbird with the file attached.
  - Quieter status messages: Saved. and Email opened.
  - Silent Markdown backup in the background on Save File.


VERSION 0.1.66
--------------
Past session recall
  - New Past Sessions button in Quick Actions.
  - Browse and search saved exports in Documents\Claim Clash Sessions\.
  - View a session preview or Use in question to ask the primary AI about a past round.

Automatic recall on Ask
  - Questions like "Didn't we ask about inflation the other day?" search saved sessions automatically.
  - Matching context is sent to the primary AI (your question text stays the same in the box).

Better export indexing
  - Exports include YAML metadata (conv, topic, date, bookmarks) for faster search.
  - Markdown backup also runs when you email an export, not only on Save File.


VERSION 0.1.67
--------------
Save File naming fix
  - Save dialog pre-fills conv number and [topic] for Markdown, Word, and PDF.
  - Topic text is stripped of HTML from the question box.
  - Windows save dialog fix for PDF, Word, and Markdown filters.


VERSION 0.1.68
--------------
Naming in all export content
  - conv N - [topic] used in file names and inside the document (title and metadata).
  - Export modal preview shows the file name before you save.


VERSION 0.1.69
--------------
Save File for all three formats
  - Save dialog pre-fills conv N - [topic] for Markdown, Word, and PDF Save File options.
  - Preview shows: Save as: filename when you click Save File.


VERSION 0.1.70
--------------
Email attach: Save to Documents first
  - Web Gmail, Yahoo, and similar browsers cannot auto-attach files (platform limit).
  - Attach file opens Save As in Documents\Claim Clash Sessions first.
  - Default name: conv N - [topic].ext (edit [topic] in the file name before saving).
  - After save, Outlook or Thunderbird opens with the file attached when installed.
  - Otherwise your email provider opens and the file is already in Documents to attach manually.


WHERE FILES ARE SAVED
---------------------
Automatic session backups (Save File and Email):
  %USERPROFILE%\Documents\Claim Clash Sessions\

Save File (your chosen location):
  Wherever you pick in the save dialog (any folder).

Email attach (Attach file option):
  Documents\Claim Clash Sessions\ first (Save As), then your mail app.
